        isDOMContentLoaded = true;

    function callOnReady(callback) {
        if (isDOMContentLoaded) callback();
        else document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', callback);
    }

    function $(argument) {
        if (typeof argument === 'function') callOnReady(argument);

        return {
            ready: callOnReady,
            load: function (callback) {
                window.addEventListener('load', callback);
            },
        };
    }

            if (loadHandler) scriptEl.addEventListener('load', loadHandler);

        })(window.globalSettings)
